   CANTO XVI	CANTO XVI

   dhyānāni catvāry adhigamya yogī prāpnoty abhijñā niyamena pañca //	DyAnAni catvAri aDigamya yogI prApnoti aBijQA niyamena paQca //
   Saund_16.1 //	SOnd-_16.1 //
   ṛddhipravekaṃ ca bahuprakāraṃ parasya cetaś caritāvabodham /	RdDi-pravekam ca bahu-prakAram parasya ca-itas carita-avaboDam /
   atītajanmasmaraṇaṃ ca dīrghaṃ divye viśuddhe śruticakṣuṣī ca // Saund_16.2	atIta-janma-smaraNam ca dIrGam divye viSudDe Sruti-cakzuzI ca // SOnd_16.2
   ataḥparaṃ tattvaparīkṣaṇena mano dadhāty āsravasaṃkṣayāya /	atas-param tattva-parIkzaNena manaH daDAti Asrava-saMkzayAya /
   tato hi duḥkhaprabhṛtīni samyak catvāri satyāni padāny avaiti //	tatas hi duHKa-praBRtIni samyak catvAri satyAni padAni avEti //
   Saund_16.3 //	SOnd-_16.3 //
   bādhātmakaṃ duḥkham idaṃ prasaktaṃ duḥkhasya hetuḥ prabhavātmako 'yam /	bADa-Atmakam duHKam idam prasaktam duHKasya hetuH praBava-AtmakaH ayam /
   duḥkhakṣayo niḥsaraṇātmako 'yaṃ trāṇātmako 'yaṃ praśamāya mārgaḥ //	duHKa-kzayaH niHsaraNa-AtmakaH ayam trANa-AtmakaH ayam praSamAya mArgaH //
   Saund_16.4 //	SOnd-_16.4 //
   ity āryasaryāny avabudhya buddhyā catvāri samyak pratividhya caiva /	iti Arya-saryAni avabuDya budDyA catvAri samyak prativiDya ca-eva /
   sarvāsravān bhāvanayābhibhūya na jāyate śāntim avāpya bhūyaḥ // Saund_16.5	sarva-AsravAn BAvanayA-aBiBUya na jAyate SAntim avApya BUyas // SOnd_16.5
   abodhato hy aprativedhataś ca tattvātmakasyāsya catuṣṭayasya /	aboDataH hi aprativeDataH ca tattva-Atmakasya-asya catuzwayasya /
   bhāvad bhavaṃ yāti na śāntim eti saṃsāradolām adhiruhya lokaḥ //	BAvat Bavam yAti na SAntim eti saMsAra-dolAm aDiruhya lokaH //
   Saund_16.6 //	SOnd-_16.6 //
   tasmāj jarāder vyasanasya mūlaṃ samāsato duḥkham avaihi janma /	tasmAt jarA-AdeH vyasanasya mUlam samAsatas duHKam avEhi janma /
   sarvauṣadhīnām iva bhūr bhavāya sarvāpadāṃ kṣetram idaṃ hi janma //	sarva-ozaDInAm iva BUH BavAya sarva-ApadAm kzetram idam hi janma //
   Saund_16.7 //	SOnd-_16.7 //

   yaḥ saṃbhavaś cāsya samucchrayasya mṛtyoṣ ca rogasya ca saṃbhavaḥ saḥ //	yaH saMBavaH ca-asya samucCrayasya mRtyoH ca rogasya ca saMBavaH saH //
   Saund_16.8 //	SOnd-_16.8 //
   sad vāpy asad vā viṣamiṣram annaṃ yathā vināśāya na dhāraṇāya /	sat vA-api asat vA vizamizram annam yaTA vinASAya na DAraNAya /
   loke tathā tiryag uparyadho vā duḥkhāya sarvaṃ na sukḥāya janma //	loke taTA tiryak upari-aDas vA duHKAya sarvam na sukHAya janma //
   Saund_16.9 //	SOnd-_16.9 //
   jarādayo naikavidhā parajānāṃ satyāṃ pravṛttau prabhavanty anarthāḥ /	jarA-AdayaH na-ekaviDA para-jAnAm satyAm pravRttO praBavanti anarTAH /
   pravātsu ghoeṣv api māruteṣu na hy aprasūtās taravaś calanti //	pravAtsu Goezu api mArutezu na hi aprasUtAH taravaH calanti //
   Saund_16.10 //	SOnd-_16.10 //

   āpo yathāntarvasudhāśayāś ca duḥkhaṃ tathā cittaśarīrayoni // Saund_16.11	ApaH yaTA-antarvasuDA-ASayAH ca duHKam taTA citta-SarIra-yoni // SOnd-_16.11
   apāṃ dravatvaṃ kaṭhinatvam urvyā vāyoś calatvaṃ dhruvam auṣṇyam agneḥ /	apAm drava-tvam kaWina-tvam urvyA vAyoH cala-tvam Druvam OzNyam agneH /
   yathā svabhāvo hi tathā svabhāvo duḥkhaṃ śarīrasya ca cetasaś ca //	yaTA svaBAvaH hi taTA svaBAvaH duHKam SarIrasya ca cetasaH ca //
   Saund_16.12 //	SOnd-_16.12 //

   rupāśrite cetasi sānubandhe śokāratikrodhabhayādi duḥkham // Saund_16.13	rupASrite cetasi sa-anubanDe Soka-arati-kroDa-Baya-Adi duHKam // SOnd_16.13

   yathā ca tad duḥkham idaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ duḥkhaṃ tathānāgatam apy avehi //	yaTA ca tat duHKam idam ca duHKam duHKam taTA-anAgatam api avehi //
   Saund_16.14 //	SOnd-_16.14 //

   Saund_16.15 //	SOnd-_16.15 //

   Saund_16.16 //	SOnd-_16.16 //

   naiveṣvaro na prakṛtir na kālo nāpi svabhāvo na vidhir yadṛcchā //	na-eva-izu-araH na prakRtiH na kAlaH na-api svaBAvaH na viDiH yadRcCA //
   Saund_16.17 //	SOnd-_16.17 //
   jñātavyam etena ca kāraṇena lokasya doṣebhya iti pravṛttiḥ /	jQAtavyam etena ca kAraNena lokasya dozeByaH iti pravRttiH /
   yasmān mriyante sarajastamaskā na jāyate vītarajastmaskaḥ // Saund_16.18	yasmAt mriyante sa-rajaH-tamaskA na jAyate vIta-rajaH-tmaskaH // SOnd-_16.18

   Saund_16.19 //	SOnd-_16.19 //
   sattvāny abhiṣvaṅgavaśāni dṛṣṭvā svajātiṣu prītiparāṇy atīva /	sattvAni aBizvaFga-vaSAni dRzwvA sva-jAtizu prIti-parANi atIva /

   phalaṃ hi yādṛk samavaiti sākṣāt tadāgamād bījam avaity atītam /	Palam hi yAdRS samavEti sAkzAt tad-AgamAt bIjam avEti atItam /

   Saund_16.24 //	SOnd-_16.24 //
   taj janmano naikavidhasya saumya tṛṣṇādayo hetava ity avetya /	tat janmanaH na-ekaviDasya sOmya tRzNA-AdayaH hetavaH iti avetya /
   tāṃś chindhi duḥkhād yadi nirmumukṣā kāryakṣayaḥ kāraṇasaṃkṣayād dhi //	tAn CinDi duHKAt yadi nirmumukzA kArya-kzayaH kAraNa-saMkzayAt Di //
   Saund_16.25 //	SOnd-_16.25 //

   Saund_16.26 //	SOnd-_16.26 //

   athaivam ādesitatattvamārgo nandas tadā prāptavimokṣamārgaḥ /	aTa-evam Adesita-tattva-mArgaH nandaH tadA prApta-vimokza-mArgaH /
   sarveṇa bhāvena gurau praṇamya kleśaprahāṇāya vanaṃ jagāma // Saund_17.1	sarveNa BAvena gurO praNamya kleSa-prahANAya vanam jagAma // SOnd_17.1
   tatrāvakāśaṃ mṛdunīlaśaṣpaṃ dadarśa sāntaṃ taruṣaṇḍavantam /	tatra-avakASam mRdu-nIla-Sazpam dadarSa sAntam taru-zaNxavantam /

   Saund_17.19 //	SOnd-_17.19 //

   sāmagryathaḥ saṃbhavati pravṛttiḥ śūnyaṃ tato lokam imaṃ dadarśa //	sAmagryaTaH saMBavati pravRttiH SUnyam tatas lokam imam dadarSa //
